FIFTH COMMITTEE 40th meeting
Pattern of conferences [124]
The representative of Austria, coordinator of informal consultations on this item, introduced and orally corrected draft resolution A/C.5/56/L.24.
The Committee adopted, without a vote, the draft resolution, as orally corrected.
Report of the Secretary-General on the activities of the Office of Internal Oversight Services [130]
The representative of Iraq made a statement.
The representative of Botswana, coordinator of informal consultations on this item, introduced draft resolution A/C.5/ 56/L.36.
Following the adoption of the draft resolution, the representative of Iraq made a statement.
Programme budget for the biennium 2000-2001 [122]
Administrative and budgetary aspects of the financing of the United Nations peacekeeping operations [133]
The Committee resumed its consideration of these agenda items.
Comprehensive review of the whole question of peace-keeping operations in all their aspects
The representative of Pakistan, coordinator of informal consultations on this question, introduced draft resolution A/C.5/56/L.32.
The representative of Algeria made a statement.
Statements in explanation of position were made by the representatives Belgium (on behalf of the European Union) and Cuba.
The Director of the Peacekeeping Financing Division introduced a note by the Secretary-General on the Support Account for peacekeeping operations (A/C.5/56/34).
On the proposal of the Chairman, the Committee decided, without a vote, to take note of document A/C.5/56/34.
The Committee thus concluded its consideration of these agenda items at this stage.
Programme budget implications
The Committee had before it draft decisions contained in document A/C.5/56/L.33.
The Committee adopted, without a vote, the draft decisions.
The representative of Guatemala made a statement.
Statements in explanation of position were made by the representatives of Israel and Cuba.
Revised estimates resulting from resolutions and decisions adopted by the Economic and Social Council at its substantive session of 2001
The Committee had before it draft decision A/C.5/56/ L.37.
Request for subvention to the United Nations Institute for Disarmament Research resulting from the recommendations of the Board of Trustees of the Institute contained in the report of the Board
The Committee had before it draft decision A/C.5/56/ L.39.
International Trade Centre UNCTAD/WTO
The Committee had before it draft decision A/C.5/56/ L.38.
Safety and security of United Nations personnel
The representative of Cuba, coordinator of informal consultations on this question, introduced draft resolution A/C.5/ 56/L.31.
Statements in explanation of position were made by the representatives of the Syrian Arab Republic and Algeria.
Report of the Secretary-General on the contingency fund: consolidated statement of programme budget implications and revised estimates
The Director of the Programme Planning and Budget Division introduced the report of the Secretary-General (A/C.5/ 56/33).
The Chairman of the Advisory Committee on Administrative and Budgetary Questions orally introduced the related report of that Committee.
On the proposal of the Chairman, the Committee decided, without a vote, to recommend that the General Assembly note that a balance of $2,192,100 remained in the contingency fund.
The representative of Cuba made a statement.
Report of the Secretary-General on the utilization of the provision for special political missions
The Director of the Programme Planning and Budget Division introduced the report of the Secretary-General (A/ C.5/56/32).
On the proposal of the Chairman, the Committee decided, without a vote, to recommend that the General Assembly approve a charge of $33,690,300 against the provision for special political missions.
The Committee continued its consideration of this agenda item.
Questions relating to the proposed programme budget for the biennium 2002-2003
The Committee had before it draft resolution A/C.5/56/ L.29 submitted by the Chairman, which was coordinated by the representative of Portugal.
Statements were made by the representatives Belgium, the Islamic Republic of Iran, Austria, Cameroon, Botswana, the Syrian Arab Republic, Ukraine, Cuba and Algeria.
The Chairman of the Advisory Committee on Administrative and Budgetary Questions and the Director of the Programme Planning and Budget Division replied to questions raised.
Statements were made by the representatives of Belgium (on behalf of the European Union), the Islamic Republic of Iran (on behalf of the Group of 77 and China), Kenya, Cuba, the Syrian Arab Republic and India.
Draft report of the Fifth Committee
The Chairman drew the attention of the Committee to the draft report and draft resolutions contained in document A/C.5/56/L.28 (Parts I and II) submitted by the Secretariat, on behalf of the Rapporteur of the Committee, Mr. Santiago Wins (Uruguay).
The Director of the Programme Planning and Budget Division orally corrected the draft report.
Statements were made by the representatives of Cuba and the Syrian Arab Republic.
The Director of the Programme Planning and Budget Division and the Chairman of the Advisory Committee on Administrative and Budgetary Questions replied to questions raised.
The Committee adopted, without a vote, the draft report and draft resolutions contained in A/C.5/56/L.28 (Parts I and II) as orally corrected.
Biennial programme of work
The Chairman introduced draft decision A/C.5/56/L.34.
Action taken on certain items
The Chairman introduced draft decision A/C.5/56/L.35 and informed the Committee that the first part of the resumed fifty-sixth session of the General Assembly would be held from 4 to 15 March 2002 and the second part from 6 to 31 May 2002.
The representative of the Syrian Arab Republic made a statement.
The Chairman made a statement.
Closure of the work of the Fifth Committee during the main part of the fifty-sixth session of the General Assembly
Statements were made by the representatives of Botswana (on behalf of the African States), Mexico (on behalf of the Latin American and Caribbean States), Latvia (on behalf of the Eastern European States), Croatia and the Islamic Republic of Iran.
The Chairman made a statement and declared the work of the Fifth Committee during the main part of the fifty-sixth session of the General Assembly concluded.
